## USER 🧑‍💻

- SubjectManager で CSV インポート時、CSV 内の順序で order が振られるようにしたい。
- この際、Subject (Middle) が変わったら、Subject (Small) の order をリセット、Subject (Large) が変わったら、Subject (Middle) の order をリセットというような階層を考えた order を振ってほしい。
- Manage Subject の画面で Subject の表示順序を変えられるインターフェースを導入したい。可能ならドラッグアンドドロップ、上下ボタンによる表示順序の変更を可能にしたい。この際も階層を考慮する。

## MODEL ✨

**Examining Reordering Logic** I'm currently focused on how reordering should function within the `SubjectManager.tsx` component, given its tree structure. The goal is to provide a smooth reordering experience that matches the functionality of `RoomManager.tsx`. I believe a strategy using drag-and-drop combined with a save method will be appropriate here, but I need to analyze how best to do this.**Considering Implementation Steps** I've outlined the necessary modifications to the backend CSV import function in `backend/src/index.ts`. I will use nested counters to preserve the proper order, specifically by tracking level changes and incrementing order values accordingly. I will now integrate this updated logic and ensure the subject ordering is maintained upon import.**Refining Backend Order Handling** I've examined the intricacies of the CSV import process. My strategy involves tracking level changes and employing nested counters, specifically `largeOrder`, `middleOrder`, and `smallOrder`. This allows for proper ordering of subjects in the tree structure based on the CSV input. I'm now fine-tuning the integration to ensure the expected subject order is accurately maintained after the import.**Evaluating Frontend Implementation** I'm now focusing on how the frontend component should handle reordering. The initial approach involves incorporating "Up" and "Down" buttons within the `renderSubjectNode` function, enabling users to adjust subject positions. A key consideration is the potential need for a "Save Order" button, similar to `RoomManager.tsx`, versus saving immediately. I am also thinking about how to integrate a `handleMoveSubject` function and how it should interact with the component's state.**Evaluating Subject Reordering Design** I'm now contemplating the user experience for reordering. Following the design of `RoomManager.tsx`, I'll implement "Up" and "Down" buttons within `renderSubjectNode`, enabling level-specific subject adjustments. I need a "Save Order" button to persist the local `subjects` changes. The frontend will fetch data, which I need to preserve. I'm investigating how native HTML5 drag-and-drop can be incorporated for sibling reordering. First, I need to look into how the import works with the CSV.**Revisiting Drag and Drop** I'm now focusing on reordering within `SubjectManager.tsx`. I'll mimic the "Up" and "Down" buttons from `RoomManager.tsx` to shift subjects. My current strategy is to enable sibling reordering using native HTML5 drag and drop, although this presents challenges with the tree structure. The backend's CSV import update for correct order is still in progress.**Defining the Reorder Plan** I've carefully reviewed the `SubjectManager.tsx` component and its data fetching. Now, I will implement both the backend CSV order update and a frontend reordering capability. The frontend will feature "Up" and "Down" buttons to adjust subject order. The design will mimic `RoomManager.tsx` and it will have a "Save Order" button. I will start with a native HTML5 drag and drop, although this introduces challenges to consider.**Evaluating Order Assignment** I'm now determining how to handle order assignment during CSV import in `backend/src/index.ts`. My plan involves utilizing nested counters – `largeOrder`, `middleOrder`, and `smallOrder` – to maintain the desired subject order based on the CSV input. I'll remove the reliance on the existing `order` field within the CSV. I need to make sure the "omission filling" logic is maintained and order is correct.**Considering Order Assignment Strategy** I'm now revisiting the CSV import logic in `backend/src/index.ts`, specifically how I can assign the correct `order` values automatically based on the CSV input. I've determined that nested counters, with `largeCount`, `middleCount`, and `smallCount`, offer the best approach for maintaining order, aligning with the hierarchical structure of the data. I'll need to reset these counters when parent levels change within the CSV data.**Revising Import and Reordering** I'm now revisiting the CSV import function, specifically within `backend/src/index.ts`. My key plan involves nested counters: `largeCount`, `middleCount`, and `smallCount`. These will ensure subjects are ordered correctly based on their CSV sequence. I'll need to reset these counters when parent levels shift to maintain a correct order. Also, I will address the frontend reordering and determine the appropriate method for subject movement.**Analyzing Component Reordering** I'm presently exploring how to structure subject reordering within the `SubjectManager.tsx` component. The `RoomManager.tsx`'s drag-and-drop combined with a save method will be appropriate here, but I need to analyze how to apply this to the tree structure.**Defining Subject Hierarchy Structure** I'm now revisiting the logic and considering how to manage level changes, specifically to ensure that the correct order is maintained, and I'll use a `largeCount`, a `middleCount`, and a `smallCount`. The frontend's reordering feature will need to sync correctly.`RoomManager.tsx` provides a template for hierarchical reordering in `SubjectManager.tsx`, using both drag-and-drop and up/down buttons with a "Save Order" button.
```json
{
  "name": "replace",
  "args": {
    "old_string": "export function SubjectManager({ backendUrl, onClose, onUpdate, labels }: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n  const [courseTypes, setCourseTypes] = useState<CourseType[]>([]);\n  const [subjects, setSubjects] = useState<Subject[]>([]);\n  const [selectedTypeId, setSelectedTypeId] = useState<string | null>(null);\n  const [editingType, setEditingType] = useState<Partial<CourseType> | null>(null);\n  const [editingSubject, setEditingSubject] = useState<Partial<Subject> | null>(null);\n  const [expandedNodes, setExpandedNodes] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set());\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    fetchData();\n  }, []);\n\n  const fetchData = async () => {\n    try {\n      const typeRes = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/course-types`, { credentials: 'include' });\n      if (typeRes.ok) {\n        const types = await typeRes.json();\n        setCourseTypes(types);\n        if (types.length > 0 && !selectedTypeId) setSelectedTypeId(types[0].id);\n      }\n      const subRes = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/subjects`, { credentials: 'include' });\n      if (subRes.ok) setSubjects(await subRes.json());\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to fetch data:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const toggleNode = (id: string) => {\n    const newExpanded = new Set(expandedNodes);\n    if (newExpanded.has(id)) newExpanded.delete(id);\n    else newExpanded.add(id);\n    setExpandedNodes(newExpanded);\n  };\n",
    "allow_multiple": false,
    "new_string": "export function SubjectManager({ backendUrl, onClose, onUpdate, labels }: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n  const [courseTypes, setCourseTypes] = useState<CourseType[]>([]);\n  const [subjects, setSubjects] = useState<Subject[]>([]);\n  const [selectedTypeId, setSelectedTypeId] = useState<string | null>(null);\n  const [editingType, setEditingType] = useState<Partial<CourseType> | null>(null);\n  const [editingSubject, setEditingSubject] = useState<Partial<Subject> | null>(null);\n  const [expandedNodes, setExpandedNodes] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set());\n  const [isModified, setIsModified] = useState(false);\n\n  // For Drag and Drop\n  const dragItemRef = useRef<{ id: string, parentId: string | null, level: number } | null>(null);\n  const dragOverItemRef = useRef<{ id: string, parentId: string | null, level: number } | null>(null);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    fetchData();\n  }, []);\n\n  const fetchData = async () => {\n    try {\n      const typeRes = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/course-types`, { credentials: 'include' });\n      if (typeRes.ok) {\n        const types = await typeRes.json();\n        setCourseTypes(types);\n        if (types.length > 0 && !selectedTypeId) setSelectedTypeId(types[0].id);\n      }\n      const subRes = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/subjects`, { credentials: 'include' });\n      if (subRes.ok) {\n        const data = await subRes.json();\n        setSubjects(data.sort((a: Subject, b: Subject) => (a.order || 0) - (b.order || 0)));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to fetch data:', err);\n    }\n    setIsModified(false);\n  };\n\n  const toggleNode = (id: string) => {\n    const newExpanded = new Set(expandedNodes);\n    if (newExpanded.has(id)) newExpanded.delete(id);\n    else newExpanded.add(id);\n    setExpandedNodes(newExpanded);\n  };\n\n  const handleMoveSubject = (subjectId: string, direction: 'up' | 'down') => {\n    const subject = subjects.find(s => s.id === subjectId);\n    if (!subject) return;\n\n    const siblings = subjects\n      .filter(s => s.parentId === subject.parentId && s.courseTypeId === subject.courseTypeId && s.level === subject.level)\n      .sort((a, b) => (a.order || 0) - (b.order || 0));\n\n    const index = siblings.findIndex(s => s.id === subjectId);\n    const targetIndex = direction === 'up' ? index - 1 : index + 1;\n\n    if (targetIndex < 0 || targetIndex >= siblings.length) return;\n\n    const newSubjects = [...subjects];\n    const targetSubject = siblings[targetIndex];\n    \n    // Swap orders\n    const tempOrder = subject.order;\n    const s1 = newSubjects.find(s => s.id === subject.id)!;\n    const s2 = newSubjects.find(s => s.id === targetSubject.id)!;\n    s1.order = targetSubject.order;\n    s2.order = tempOrder;\n\n    setSubjects(newSubjects.sort((a, b) => (a.order || 0) - (b.order || 0)));\n    setIsModified(true);\n  };\n\n  const handleDragStart = (subject: Subject) => {\n    dragItemRef.current = { id: subject.id, parentId: subject.parentId, level: subject.level };\n  };\n\n  const handleDragEnter = (subject: Subject) => {\n    // Only allow drag over siblings\n    if (dragItemRef.current && \n        dragItemRef.current.parentId === subject.parentId && \n        dragItemRef.current.level === subject.level &&\n        dragItemRef.current.id !== subject.id) {\n      dragOverItemRef.current = { id: subject.id, parentId: subject.parentId, level: subject.level };\n    } else {\n      dragOverItemRef.current = null;\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleDragEnd = () => {\n    if (!dragItemRef.current || !dragOverItemRef.current) {\n      dragItemRef.current = null;\n      dragOverItemRef.current = null;\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const newSubjects = [...subjects];\n    const siblings = newSubjects\n      .filter(s => s.parentId === dragItemRef.current!.parentId && s.courseTypeId === selectedTypeId && s.level === dragItemRef.current!.level)\n      .sort((a, b) => (a.order || 0) - (b.order || 0));\n\n    const fromIdx = siblings.findIndex(s => s.id === dragItemRef.current!.id);\n    const toIdx = siblings.findIndex(s => s.id === dragOverItemRef.current!.id);\n\n    const [movedItem] = siblings.splice(fromIdx, 1);\n    siblings.splice(toIdx, 0, movedItem);\n\n    // Re-assign orders based on new sequence\n    siblings.forEach((s, idx) => {\n      const original = newSubjects.find(ns => ns.id === s.id)!;\n      original.order = idx + 1;\n    });\n\n    setSubjects(newSubjects.sort((a, b) => (a.order || 0) - (b.order || 0)));\n    setIsModified(true);\n    dragItemRef.current = null;\n    dragOverItemRef.current = null;\n  };\n\n  const handleSaveOrder = async () => {\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/subjects/reorder`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          orders: subjects.map(s => ({ id: s.id, order: s.order }))\n        })\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        alert(t('Order saved successfully'));\n        setIsModified(false);\n        onUpdate();\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to save order'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error saving subject order:', err);\n    }\n  };\n",
```

## MODEL ✨

**Analyzing the Changes** The code changes appear sound. I'm focusing on their implications within the broader system. Currently assessing potential side effects and performance impacts before moving forward with a full review.Changes look good.

I have implemented the hierarchical reordering interface for subjects and updated the CSV import logic.

### Summary of Changes

#### 1. Backend (CSV Import)
- Modified `backend/src/index.ts` to automatically assign hierarchical `order` values during CSV import.
- The `order` is now determined by the sequence of rows in the CSV, resetting lower-level counters when a higher-level subject changes.

#### 2. Frontend (Subject Manager UI)
- **Reordering Interface:** Added Up/Down buttons and Drag & Drop functionality to the subject tree.
- **Hierarchical Integrity:** Reordering is restricted to siblings (same parent and level) to maintain the tree structure.
- **Batch Saving:** Introduced a "Save Order" button that appears after reordering, allowing all changes to be persisted at once.
- **Visual Feedback:** Added drag handles and updated the CSS to provide a better user experience for reordering.
- **Data Synchronization:** Added an `onUpdate` prop to `SubjectManager` to ensure the main application view refreshes after changes.
- **Type Safety:** Fixed TypeScript errors related to hierarchical parent ID management.

These changes provide a more intuitive and flexible way to manage the display order of subjects while ensuring data consistency during bulk imports.

I'm focusing on "Main Teacher" and "Sub Teacher" roles to ensure data accuracy.**Mapping Out the Implementation** I'm translating the feature request into actionable steps. row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(2).value = row.level === 2 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(3).value = row.level === 3 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(4).value = row.assigned;\n        xlRow.getCell(5).value = row.scheduled;\n        xlRow.getCell(6).value = row.scheduled - row.assigned;\n        const isGroup = row.children && row.children.length > 0;\n        if (isGroup || row.level === 1) {\n          xlRow.font = { bold: true };\n          for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) xlRow.getCell(i).fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: row.level === 1 ? 'FFF5F5F5' : 'FFF9F9F9' } };\n        }\n        if (row.level === 1) { totalAssigned += row.assigned; totalScheduled += row.scheduled; }\n        for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n          const cell = xlRow.getCell(i);\n          cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n          if (i >= 4) cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'right' };\n        }\n        currentRowIdx++;\n        if (row.children) addRows(row.children);\n      });\n    };\n    addRows(stats);\n    const footerRow = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n    footerRow.getCell(1).value = t('Grand Total');\n    worksheet.mergeCells(currentRowIdx, 1, currentRowIdx, 3);\n    footerRow.getCell(4).value = totalAssigned;\n    footerRow.getCell(5).value = totalScheduled;\n    footerRow.getCell(6).value = totalScheduled - totalAssigned;\n    footerRow.font = { bold: true };\n    for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n      const cell = footerRow.getCell(i);\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'medium' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'medium' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n      if (i >= 4) cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'right' };\n    }\n    const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n    saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), `Statistics_${courseName}_${format(new Date(), 'yyyyMMdd')}.xlsx`);\n  } catch (err) { console.error('Course Statistics Export Error:', err); }\n}\n"

text-align: right; font-weight: bold; }\n\n.stat-group {\n  background: #2a2a2a;\n  font-weight: bold;\n}\n\n.course-subtotal {\n  background: #333;\n  font-weight: bold;\n}\n\n.grand-total {\n  background: #444;\n  font-weight: bold;\n  font-size: 1rem;\n}\n\n@media (prefers-color-scheme: light) {\n  .teacher-statistics-box { background: #fff; color: #333; }\n  .range-selector { background: #f5f5f5; }\n  .range-selector input { background: #fff; border-color: #ccc; color: #333; }\n  .stat-table th { background: #f0f0f0; }\n  .stat-table th, .stat-table td { border-color: #eee; ## MODEL ✨

I'll build `TeacherStatistics.tsx` to group lessons by course and subject hierarchy, then calculate the total hours for each. I'll include date range filters and an Excel export feature, ensuring the logic handles multi-day lessons and correctly assigns credits to main and sub-teachers. I'll then move on to adding the Excel export function to `src/utils/excelExport.ts`.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "import { useState, useMemo } from 'preact/hooks';\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';\nimport { CourseType, Subject, Lesson, TimePeriod, ResourceLabels, Resource } from '../types';\nimport { parseISO, differenceInDays, isWithinInterval, startOfDay, endOfDay } from 'date-fns';\nimport { exportTeacherStatisticsToExcel } from '../utils/excelExport';\nimport './TeacherStatistics.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  teacher: Resource;\n  courses: Resource[];\n  subjects: Subject[];\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  onClose: () => void;\n  initialStartDate?: string;\n  initialEndDate?: string;\n}\n\ninterface TeacherStatRow {\n  courseId: string;\n  courseName: string;\n  largeSubject: string;\n  middleSubject: string;\n  smallSubject: string;\n  mainHours: number;\n  subHours: number;\n  totalHours: number;\n  level: number; // 1: Course, 2: Subject Row, 3: Course Subtotal\n}\n\nexport function TeacherStatistics({ \n  teacher, courses, subjects, lessons, periods, labels, onClose, \n  initialStartDate, initialEndDate \n}: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n  const [startDate, setStartDate] = useState(initialStartDate || '');\n  const [endDate, setEndDate] = useState(initialEndDate || '');\n\n  const calculatePeriods = (l: Lesson) => {\n    const sIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n    const eIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n    if (sIdx === -1 || eIdx === -1) return 0;\n\n    if (l.startDate === l.endDate) {\n      return eIdx - sIdx + 1;\n    } else {\n      const numDays = differenceInDays(parseISO(l.endDate), parseISO(l.startDate));\n      return (periods.length - sIdx) + (numDays - 1) * periods.length + (eIdx + 1);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const stats = useMemo(() => {\n    // 1. Filter lessons by date range and teacher\n    const filteredLessons = lessons.filter(l => {\n      const lessonStart = parseISO(l.startDate);\n      const lessonEnd = parseISO(l.endDate);\n      \n      // Teacher filter\n      const isMain = l.teacherId === teacher.id;\n      const isSub = l.subTeacherIds?.includes(teacher.id) || l.subTeachers?.some(st => st.id === teacher.id);\n      if (!isMain && !isSub) return false;\n\n      // Date filter\n      if (startDate && lessonEnd < parseISO(startDate)) return false;\n      if (endDate && lessonStart > parseISO(endDate)) return false;\n\n      return true;\n    });\n\n    // 2. Group by Course and Subject\n    const groupedData: Record<string, Record<string, { main: number, sub: number }>> = {};\n\n    filteredLessons.forEach(l => {\n      const course = courses.find(c => c.id === l.courseId);\n      if (!course) return;\n\n      const courseKey = course.id;\n      if (!groupedData[courseKey]) groupedData[courseKey] = {};\n\n      const subject = subjects.find(s => s.id === l.subjectId);\n      const subjectKey = subject ? subject.id : (l.subjectId || 'unknown');\n      \n      if (!groupedData[courseKey][subjectKey]) {\n        groupedData[courseKey][subjectKey] = { main: 0, sub: 0 };\n      }\n\n      const hours = calculatePeriods(l);\n      if (l.teacherId === teacher.id) {\n        groupedData[courseKey][subjectKey].main += hours;\n      } else {\n        groupedData[courseKey][subjectKey].sub += hours;\n      }\n    });\n\n    // 3. Flatten and build hierarchy\n    const rows: TeacherStatRow[] = [];\n    let grandTotalMain = 0;\n    let grandTotalSub = 0;\n\n    Object.entries(groupedData).forEach(([courseId, subjectGroups]) => {\n      const course = courses.find(c => c.id === courseId)!;\n      let courseTotalMain = 0;\n      let courseTotalSub = 0;\n\n      // Group subjects by their hierarchy\n      const courseRows: TeacherStatRow[] = [];\n\n      Object.entries(subjectGroups).forEach(([subjectId, hours]) => {\n        const subject = subjects.find(s => s.id === subjectId);\n        \n        let large = '';\n        let middle = '';\n        let small = '';\n\n        if (subject) {\n          if (subject.level === 3) {\n            small = subject.name;\n            const mid = subjects.find(s => s.id === subject.parentId);\n            if (mid) {\n              middle = mid.name;\n              const lrg = subjects.find(s => s.id === mid.parentId);\n              if (lrg) large = lrg.name;\n            }\n          } else if (subject.level === 2) {\n            middle = subject.name;\n            const lrg = subjects.find(s => s.id === subject.parentId);\n            if (lrg) large = lrg.name;\n          } else if (subject.level === 1) {\n            large = subject.name;\n          }\n        } else {\n          large = subjectId; // Fallback\n        }\n\n        courseRows.push({\n          courseId,\n          courseName: course.name,\n          largeSubject: large,\n          middleSubject: middle,\n          smallSubject: small,\n          mainHours: hours.main,\n          subHours: hours.sub,\n          totalHours: hours.main + hours.sub,\n          level: 2\n        });\n\n        courseTotalMain += hours.main;\n        courseTotalSub += hours.sub;\n      });\n\n      // Sort subjects: Large -> Middle -> Small\n      courseRows.sort((a, b) => \n        a.largeSubject.localeCompare(b.largeSubject) || \n        a.middleSubject.localeCompare(b.middleSubject) || \n        a.smallSubject.localeCompare(b.smallSubject)\n      );\n\n      // Add Course Header (optional, but requested Course subtotal)\n      // Actually, standard is Course | Subject | Main | Sub | Total\n      // Let's add all subject rows, then a Course subtotal row.\n      \n      rows.push(...courseRows);\n\n      rows.push({\n        courseId,\n        courseName: course.name,\n        largeSubject: '',\n        middleSubject: '',\n        smallSubject: t('Course Subtotal'),\n        mainHours: courseTotalMain,\n        subHours: courseTotalSub,\n        totalHours: courseTotalMain + courseTotalSub,\n        level: 3\n      });\n\n      grandTotalMain += courseTotalMain;\n      grandTotalSub += courseTotalSub;\n    });\n\n    return { rows, grandTotalMain, grandTotalSub };\n  }, [teacher, courses, subjects, lessons, periods, startDate, endDate]);\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"teacher-statistics-overlay\">\n      <div className=\"teacher-statistics-box\">\n        <div className=\"dialog-header\">\n          <h2>{t('Teacher Statistics')}: {teacher.name}</h2>\n          <div className=\"header-actions\">\n            <button \n              className=\"excel-export-btn\" \n              onClick={() => exportTeacherStatisticsToExcel({ \n                teacherName: teacher.name, \n                stats: stats.rows, \n                grandTotalMain: stats.grandTotalMain,\n                grandTotalSub: stats.grandTotalSub,\n                labels, t,\n                dateRange: startDate || endDate ? `${startDate} ~ ${endDate}` : t('All Period')\n              })}\n              title={t('Export to Excel')}\n              style={{ marginRight: '10px' }}\n            >\n              <svg width=\"18\" height=\"18\" viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\" fill=\"none\" stroke=\"currentColor\" stroke-width=\"2\" stroke-linecap=\"round\" stroke-linejoin=\"round\">\n                <path d=\"M21 15v4a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2v-4\"></path>\n                <polyline points=\"7 10 12 15 17 10\"></polyline>\n                <line x1=\"12\" y1=\"15\" x2=\"12\" y2=\"3\"></line>\n              </svg>\n              <span style={{ marginLeft: '5px' }}>Excel</span>\n            </button>\n            <button className=\"close-button\" onClick={onClose}>×</button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"teacher-statistics-content\">\n          <div className=\"range-selector\">\n            <label>{t('Period')}:</label>\n            <input type=\"date\" value={startDate} onChange={e => setStartDate(e.currentTarget.value)} />\n            <span>~</span>\n            <input type=\"date\" value={endDate} onChange={e => setEndDate(e.currentTarget.value)} />\n          </div>\n\n          <table className=\"stat-table\">\n            <thead>\n              <tr>\n                <th className=\"col-course\">{labels.course}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-large\">{labels.subjectLarge}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-middle\">{labels.subjectMiddle}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-small\">{labels.subjectSmall}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-main\">{labels.mainTeacher}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-sub\">{labels.subTeacher}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-total\">{t('Subtotal')}</th>\n              </tr>\n            </thead>\n            <tbody>\n              {stats.rows.map((row, idx) => {\n                const isFirstCourseRow = idx === 0 || stats.rows[idx-1].courseId !== row.courseId;\n                return (\n                  <tr key={`${row.courseId}-${idx}`} className={row.level === 3 ? 'course-subtotal' : ''}>\n                    <td className=\"col-course\">{isFirstCourseRow ? row.courseName : ''}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-large\">{row.largeSubject}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-middle\">{row.middleSubject}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-small\">{row.smallSubject}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-main\">{row.mainHours}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-sub\">{row.subHours}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-total\">{row.totalHours}</td>\n                  </tr>\n                );\n              })}\n            </tbody>\n            <tfoot>\n              <tr className=\"grand-total\">\n                <td colSpan={4}>{t('Grand Total')}</td>\n                <td className=\"col-main\">{stats.grandTotalMain}</td>\n                <td className=\"col-sub\">{stats.grandTotalSub}</td>\n                <td className=\"col-total\">{stats.grandTotalMain + stats.grandTotalSub}</td>\n              </tr>\n            </tfoot>\n          </table>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"dialog-footer\">\n          <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={onClose}>{t('Close')}</button>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n",
    "file_path": "src/components/TeacherStatistics.tsx"
  },
  "id": "write_file_1776679100135_0"
}
```

'course-subtotal' : ''}>\n                    <td className=\"col-course\">{isFirstCourseRow ? row.courseName : ''}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-large\">{row.largeSubject}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-middle\">{row.middleSubject}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-small\">{row.smallSubject}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-main\">{row.mainHours}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-sub\">{row.subHours}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-total\">{row.totalHours}</td>\n                  </tr>\n                );\n              })}\n            </tbody>\n            <tfoot>\n              <tr className=\"grand-total\">\n                <td colSpan={4}>{t('Grand Total')}</td>\n                <td className=\"col-main\">{stats.grandTotalMain}</td>\n                <td className=\"col-sub\">{stats.grandTotalSub}</td>\n                <td className=\"col-total\">{stats.grandTotalMain + stats.grandTotalSub}</td>\n              </tr>\n            </tfoot>\n          </table>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"dialog-footer\">\n          <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={onClose}>{t('Close')}</button>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"

 if (theme) return theme;\n    // Fallback to default\n    return colorThemes.find(t => t.category === category && t.key === 'default');\n  };\n\n  const getHolidayOrWeekendTheme = (date: Date) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const dayInfo = getDayInfo(date.getDay());\n    \n    // 週末設定がある場合は、休日であっても週末のテーマを優先する\n    if (dayInfo.isWeekend) {\n      return getThemeColor('HOLIDAY', dayInfo.themeId);\n    }\n\n    // 週末でない平日の休日の場合は、holidayTheme を使用する\n    if (holiday) {\n      return getThemeColor('HOLIDAY', holidayTheme);\n    }\n    \n    return null;\n  };\n"

- Updated `GEMINI.md` to include "講師別の割当統計" (Teacher Statistics) in the list of features.

#### 2. Frontend Components
- **`TeacherStatistics.tsx` & `.css`**: Created a new modal component that calculates and displays lesson allocations for a specific teacher.
    - Groups data by Course and Subject Hierarchy (Large, Middle, Small).
    - Distinguishes between "Main Teacher" and "Sub Teacher" hours.
    - Provides subtotals per Course and a Grand Total.
    - Includes date range selectors to filter statistics (defaulting to the current view period).
- **`Timetable.tsx`**: Added a statistics button in the resource label column specifically for the Teacher View.
- **`App.tsx`**: Integrated the new component with appropriate signals (`showTeacherStatistics`, `selectedTeacherIdForStats`) and handle callbacks.

#### 3. Excel Export
- **`src/utils/excelExport.ts`**: Implemented `exportTeacherStatisticsToExcel` to generate a formatted `.xlsx` file mirroring the on-screen statistics, including grouping styles and totals.

#### 4. Internationalization
- Added translations for both Japanese and English in `public/locales/*/translation.json`.
    - New keys: `Teacher Statistics`, `Subtotal`, `All Period`, `Course Subtotal`, `Export to Excel`.

These changes allow administrators and teachers to track workload and allocation across different courses and subjects within a flexible time frame.

## MODEL ✨

`Timetable.tsx`'s `getDayCount` and `displayDates` are calculated internally, based on `baseDate`, `viewType`, and `systemSettings`. My statistics range calculation in `App.tsx` is simplified and potentially inconsistent. I should refactor `Timetable.tsx` to export a `calculateViewRange` helper or duplicate the logic in `App.tsx` using `systemSettings` and `viewType`. Given `Timetable.tsx` is large, I'll review its structure to determine the best way to extract or reuse this logic.**Tool Command**:

});\n  const weekdayFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat(locale, { weekday: 'short' });\n\n  const showFilterPopup = useSignal(false);\n  const hiddenResourceIds = useSignal<Set<string>>(new Set());\n\n  const getResourceName = (id: string) => {\n    const res = resources.find(r => r.id === id);\n    return res ? t(res.name) : id;\n  };\n\n  const currentViewStart = startOfDay(baseDate);\n\n  const getDayInfo = (day: number) => {\n    const weekendDaysStr = systemSettings?.weekendDays || \"0:default:true,1:default:false,2:default:false,3:default:false,4:default:false,5:default:false,6:vivid:true\";\n    const parts = weekendDaysStr.split(',').filter(p => p !== '');\n    const part = parts.find(p => p.startsWith(`${day}:`));\n    if (part) {\n      const bits = part.split(':');\n      if (bits.length >= 3) {\n        return { themeId: bits[1], isWeekend: bits[2] === 'true' };\n      }\n      if (bits.length === 2) {\n        return { themeId: bits[1], isWeekend: true };\n      }\n    }\n    const simpleIndices = weekendDaysStr.split(',').filter(p => !p.includes(':'));\n    if (simpleIndices.includes(day.toString())) {\n      return { themeId: 'default', isWeekend: true };\n    }\n    return { themeId: 'default', isWeekend: false };\n  };\n\n  const isWeekend = (date: Date) => getDayInfo(date.getDay()).isWeekend;\n  const holidayTheme = systemSettings?.holidayTheme || 'default';\n\n  // カラーテーマ取得用ヘルパー\n  const getThemeColor = (category: ColorCategory, keyOrId: string) => {\n    const theme = colorThemes.find(t => t.category === category && (t.key === keyOrId || t.id === keyOrId));\n    if (theme) return theme;\n    // Fallback to default\n    return colorThemes.find(t => t.category === category && t.key === 'default');\n  };\n\n  const getHolidayOrWeekendTheme = (date: Date) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const dayInfo = getDayInfo(date.getDay());\n    \n    // 週末設定がある場合は、休日であっても週末のテーマを優先する\n    if (dayInfo.isWeekend) {\n      return getThemeColor('HOLIDAY', dayInfo.themeId);\n    }\n\n    // 週末でない平日の休日の場合は、holidayTheme を使用する\n    if (holiday) {\n      return getThemeColor('HOLIDAY', holidayTheme);\n    }\n    \n    return null;\n  };\n\n  const getHoliday = (date: Date) => {\n    const targetStr = format(date, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n    return holidays.find(h => {\n      if (h.date) return h.date === targetStr;\n      if (h.start && h.end) {\n        return targetStr >= h.start && targetStr <= h.end;\n      }\n      return false;\n    });\n  };\n\n  const getDayCount = () => {\n    if (viewType === 'day') return 1;\n    if (viewType === 'week') return 7;\n    if (viewType === 'month') {\n      return differenceInDays(addMonths(currentViewStart, 1), currentViewStart);\n    }\n    if (viewType === '3month' || viewType === '6month') {\n      const months = viewType === '3month' ? 3 : 6;\n      return differenceInDays(addMonths(currentViewStart, months), currentViewStart);\n    }\n    if (viewType === 'year' || viewType === 'course_timeline') {\n      const month = systemSettings?.yearViewStartMonth ?? 4;\n      const day = systemSettings?.yearViewStartDay ?? 1;\n      \n      const start = new Date(getYear(baseDate), month - 1, day);\n      const end = new Date(getYear(baseDate) + 1, month - 1, day);\n      return differenceInDays(end, start);\n    }\n    return 1;\n  };\n\n  const dayCount = getDayCount();\n  const displayDates = Array.from({ length: dayCount }).map((_, i) => addDays(currentViewStart, i));\n  const currentViewEnd = startOfDay(displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]);\n\n  const viewStartStr = format(currentViewStart, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n  const viewEndStr = format(currentViewEnd, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n\n  const allResourcesOfMode = resources\n    .filter(r => {\n      if (r.type !== viewMode) return false;\n      // 講座ビューの場合、表示期間内に開催されているもののみを表示\n      if (viewMode === 'course') {\n        if (r.startDate && r.endDate) {\n          return r.startDate <= viewEndStr && r.endDate >= viewStartStr;\n        }\n      }\n      return true;"
```json
  }
```
```json
}
```

    "output": "import { useMemo } from 'preact/hooks';\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';\nimport { CourseType, Subject, Lesson, TimePeriod, ResourceLabels, Resource } from '../types';\nimport { parseISO, differenceInDays } from 'date-fns';\nimport { exportCourseStatisticsToExcel } from '../utils/excelExport';\nimport './CourseStatistics.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  course: Resource;\n  subjects: Subject[];\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  onClose: () => void;\n}\n\ninterface StatRow {\n  id: string;\n  name: string;\n  level: number;\n  assigned: number;\n  scheduled: number;\n  children: StatRow[];\n}\n\nexport function CourseStatistics({ course, subjects, lessons, periods, labels, onClose }: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n\n  const calculatePeriods = (l: Lesson) => {\n    const sIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n    const eIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n    if (sIdx === -1 || eIdx === -1) return 0;\n\n    if (l.startDate === l.endDate) {\n      return eIdx - sIdx + 1;\n    } else {\n      const numDays = differenceInDays(parseISO(l.endDate), parseISO(l.startDate));\n      return (periods.length - sIdx) + (numDays - 1) * periods.length + (eIdx + 1);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const stats = useMemo(() => {\n    if (!course.courseTypeId) return [];\n\n    const typeSubjects = subjects.filter(s => s.courseTypeId === course.courseTypeId);\n    const courseLessons = lessons.filter(l => l.courseId === course.id);\n\n    const buildStatTree = (parentId: string | null, level: number): StatRow[] => {\n      return typeSubjects\n        .filter(s => s.parentId === parentId)\n        .sort((a, b) => (a.order || 0) - (b.order || 0))\n        .map(s => {\n          const children = buildStatTree(s.id, level + 1);\n          \n          let assigned = 0;\n          let scheduled = 0;\n\n          if (children.length > 0) {\n            // Aggregate from children\n            assigned = children.reduce((sum, child) => sum + child.assigned, 0);\n            scheduled = children.reduce((sum, child) => sum + child.scheduled, 0);\n          } else {\n            // Leaf node: get assigned from course.subjects and scheduled from courseLessons\n            const courseSub = course.subjects?.find(cs => cs.subjectId === s.id);\n            assigned = courseSub?.totalPeriods || 0;\n            \n            scheduled = courseLessons\n              .filter(l => l.subjectId === s.id || (l.subjectId === null && l.subject === s.name))\n              .reduce((sum, l) => sum + calculatePeriods(l), 0);\n          }\n\n          return {\n            id: s.id,\n            name: s.name,\n            level: s.level,\n            assigned,\n            scheduled,\n            children\n          };\n        });\n    };\n\n    return buildStatTree(null, 1);\n  }, [course, subjects, lessons, periods]);\n\n  const grandTotalAssigned = stats.reduce((sum, row) => sum + row.assigned, 0);\n  const grandTotalScheduled = stats.reduce((sum, row) => sum + row.scheduled, 0);\n\n  const renderRows = (rows: StatRow[]) => {\n    const elements: any[] = [];\n\n    const traverse = (row: StatRow) => {\n      elements.push(\n        <tr key={row.id} className={`stat-level-${row.level} ${row.children.length > 0 ? 'stat-group' : 'stat-leaf'}`}>\n          <td className=\"col-large\">{row.level === 1 ? row.name : ''}</td>\n          <td className=\"col-middle\">{row.level === 2 ? row.name : ''}</td>\n          <td className=\"col-small\">{row.level === 3 ? row.name : ''}</td>\n          <td className=\"col-assigned\">{row.assigned}</td>\n          <td className=\"col-scheduled\">{row.scheduled}</td>\n          <td className=\"col-diff\">\n            <span className={row.scheduled > row.assigned ? 'text-over' : row.scheduled < row.assigned ? 'text-under' : ''}>\n              {row.scheduled - row.assigned}\n            </span>\n          </td>\n        </tr>\n      );\n      row.children.forEach(traverse);\n    };\n\n    rows.forEach(traverse);\n    return elements;\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"course-statistics-overlay\">\n      <div className=\"course-statistics-box\">\n        <div className=\"dialog-header\">\n          <h2>{t('Course Statistics')}: {course.name}</h2>\n          <div className=\"header-actions\">\n            <button \n              className=\"excel-export-btn\" \n              onClick={() => exportCourseStatisticsToExcel({ courseName: course.name, stats, labels, t })}\n              title={t('Export to Excel')}\n              style={{ marginRight: '10px' }}\n            >\n              <svg width=\"18\" height=\"18\" viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\" fill=\"none\" stroke=\"currentColor\" stroke-width=\"2\" stroke-linecap=\"round\" stroke-linejoin=\"round\">\n                <path d=\"M21 15v4a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2v-4\"></path>\n                <polyline points=\"7 10 12 15 17 10\"></polyline>\n                <line x1=\"12\" y1=\"15\" x2=\"12\" y2=\"3\"></line>\n              </svg>\n              <span style={{ marginLeft: '5px' }}>Excel</span>\n            </button>\n            <button className=\"close-button\" onClick={onClose}>×</button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"course-statistics-content\">\n          <table className=\"stat-table\">\n            <thead>\n              <tr>\n                <th className=\"col-large\">{labels.subjectLarge}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-middle\">{labels.subjectMiddle}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-small\">{labels.subjectSmall}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-assigned\">{t('Assigned')}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-scheduled\">{t('Scheduled')}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-diff\">{t('Diff')}</th>\n              </tr>\n            </thead>\n            <tbody>\n              {renderRows(stats)}\n            </tbody>\n            <tfoot>\n              <tr className=\"grand-total\">\n                <td colSpan={3}>{t('Grand Total')}</td>\n                <td className=\"col-assigned\">{grandTotalAssigned}</td>\n                <td className=\"col-scheduled\">{grandTotalScheduled}</td>\n                <td className=\"col-diff\">{grandTotalScheduled - grandTotalAssigned}</td>\n              </tr>\n            </tfoot>\n  );\n}\n"

For example, to read the next section of the file, use start_line: 1086.\n\n--- FILE CONTENT (truncated) ---\nexport async function exportCourseStatisticsToExcel({\n  courseName, stats, labels, t\n}: {\n  courseName: string;\n  stats: any[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  t: (key: string, options?: any) => string;\n}) {\n  try {\n    const workbook = new ExcelJS.Workbook();\n    const worksheet = workbook.addWorksheet('Statistics');\n    worksheet.mergeCells(1, 1, 1, 6);\n    const titleCell = worksheet.getCell(1, 1);\n    titleCell.value = `${t('Course Statistics')}: ${courseName}`;\n    titleCell.font = { bold: true, size: 14 };\n    titleCell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };\n    const headers = [labels.subjectLarge, labels.subjectMiddle, labels.subjectSmall, t('Assigned'), t('Scheduled'), t('Diff')];\n    const headerRow = worksheet.getRow(3);\n    headers.forEach((h, i) => {\n      const cell = headerRow.getCell(i + 1);\n      cell.value = h;\n      cell.font = { bold: true };\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n      cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };\n    });\n    worksheet.getColumn(1).width = 25; worksheet.getColumn(2).width = 25; worksheet.getColumn(3).width = 30;\n    worksheet.getColumn(4).width = 12; worksheet.getColumn(5).width = 12; worksheet.getColumn(6).width = 12;\n    let currentRowIdx = 4;\n    let totalAssigned = 0;\n    let totalScheduled = 0;\n    const addRows = (rows: any[]) => {\n      rows.forEach(row => {\n        const xlRow = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n        xlRow.getCell(1).value = row.level === 1 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(2).value = row.level === 2 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(3).value = row.level === 3 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(4).value = row.assigned;\n        xlRow.getCell(5).value = row.scheduled;\n        xlRow.getCell(6).value = row.scheduled - row.assigned;\n        const isGroup = row.children && row.children.length > 0;\n        if (isGroup || row.level === 1) {\n          xlRow.font = { bold: true };\n          for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) xlRow.getCell(i).fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: row.level === 1 ? 'FFF5F5F5' : 'FFF9F9F9' } };\n        }\n        if (row.level === 1) { totalAssigned += row.assigned; totalScheduled += row.scheduled; }\n        for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n          const cell = xlRow.getCell(i);\n          cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n          if (i >= 4) cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'right' };\n        }\n        currentRowIdx++;\n        if (row.children) addRows(row.children);\n      });\n    };\n    addRows(stats);\n    const footerRow = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n    footerRow.getCell(1).value = t('Grand Total');\n    worksheet.mergeCells(currentRowIdx, 1, currentRowIdx, 3);\n    footerRow.getCell(4).value = totalAssigned;\n    footerRow.getCell(5).value = totalScheduled;\n    footerRow.getCell(6).value = totalScheduled - totalAssigned;\n    footerRow.font = { bold: true };\n    for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n      const cell = footerRow.getCell(i);\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'medium' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'medium' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n      if (i >= 4) cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'right' };\n    }\n    const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n    saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), `Statistics_${courseName}_${format(new Date(), 'yyyyMMdd')}.xlsx`);\n  } catch (err) { console.error('Course Statistics Export Error:', err); }\n}\n"

## USER 🧑‍💻

**Tool Response**:
```json
{
  "id": "read_file_1776680480998_0",
  "name": "read_file",
  "response": {
    "output": "import { useState, useMemo } from 'preact/hooks';\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';\nimport { CourseType, Subject, Lesson, TimePeriod, ResourceLabels, Resource } from '../types';\nimport { parseISO, differenceInDays, isWithinInterval, startOfDay, endOfDay } from 'date-fns';\nimport { exportTeacherStatisticsToExcel } from '../utils/excelExport';\nimport './TeacherStatistics.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  teacher: Resource;\n  courses: Resource[];\n  subjects: Subject[];\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  onClose: () => void;\n  initialStartDate?: string;\n  initialEndDate?: string;\n}\n\ninterface TeacherStatRow {\n  courseId: string;\n  courseName: string;\n  largeSubject: string;\n  middleSubject: string;\n  smallSubject: string;\n  mainHours: number;\n  subHours: number;\n  totalHours: number;\n  level: number; // 1: Course, 2: Subject Row, 3: Course Subtotal\n}\n\nexport function TeacherStatistics({ \n  teacher, courses, subjects, lessons, periods, labels, onClose, \n  initialStartDate, initialEndDate \n}: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n  const [startDate, setStartDate] = useState(initialStartDate || '');\n  const [endDate, setEndDate] = useState(initialEndDate || '');\n\n  const calculatePeriods = (l: Lesson) => {\n    const sIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n    const eIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n    if (sIdx === -1 || eIdx === -1) return 0;\n\n    if (l.startDate === l.endDate) {\n      return eIdx - sIdx + 1;\n    } else {\n      const numDays = differenceInDays(parseISO(l.endDate), parseISO(l.startDate));\n      return (periods.length - sIdx) + (numDays - 1) * periods.length + (eIdx + 1);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const stats = useMemo(() => {\n    // 1. Filter lessons by date range and teacher\n    const filteredLessons = lessons.filter(l => {\n      const lessonStart = parseISO(l.startDate);\n      const lessonEnd = parseISO(l.endDate);\n      \n      // Teacher filter\n      const isMain = l.teacherId === teacher.id;\n      const isSub = l.subTeacherIds?.includes(teacher.id) || l.subTeachers?.some(st => st.id === teacher.id);\n      if (!isMain && !isSub) return false;\n\n      // Date filter\n      if (startDate && lessonEnd < parseISO(startDate)) return false;\n      if (endDate && lessonStart > parseISO(endDate)) return false;\n\n      return true;\n    });\n\n    // 2. Group by Course and Subject\n    const groupedData: Record<string, Record<string, { main: number, sub: number }>> = {};\n\n    filteredLessons.forEach(l => {\n      const course = courses.find(c => c.id === l.courseId);\n      if (!course) return;\n\n      const courseKey = course.id;\n      if (!groupedData[courseKey]) groupedData[courseKey] = {};\n\n      const subject = subjects.find(s => s.id === l.subjectId);\n      const subjectKey = subject ? subject.id : (l.subjectId || 'unknown');\n      \n      if (!groupedData[courseKey][subjectKey]) {\n        groupedData[courseKey][subjectKey] = { main: 0, sub: 0 };\n      }\n\n      const hours = calculatePeriods(l);\n      if (l.teacherId === teacher.id) {\n        groupedData[courseKey][subjectKey].main += hours;\n      } else {\n        groupedData[courseKey][subjectKey].sub += hours;\n      }\n    });\n\n    // 3. Flatten and build hierarchy\n    const rows: TeacherStatRow[] = [];\n    let grandTotalMain = 0;\n    let grandTotalSub = 0;\n\n    Object.entries(groupedData).forEach(([courseId, subjectGroups]) => {\n      const course = courses.find(c => c.id === courseId)!;\n      let courseTotalMain = 0;\n      let courseTotalSub = 0;\n\n      // Group subjects by their hierarchy\n      const courseRows: TeacherStatRow[] = [];\n\n      Object.entries(subjectGroups).forEach(([subjectId, hours]) => {\n        const subject = subjects.find(s => s.id === subjectId);\n        \n        let large = '';\n        let middle = '';\n        let small = '';\n\n        if (subject) {\n          if (subject.level === 3) {\n            small = subject.name;\n            const mid = subjects.find(s => s.id === subject.parentId);\n            if (mid) {\n              middle = mid.name;\n              const lrg = subjects.find(s => s.id === mid.parentId);\n              if (lrg) large = lrg.name;\n            }\n          } else if (subject.level === 2) {\n            middle = subject.name;\n            const lrg = subjects.find(s => s.id === subject.parentId);\n            if (lrg) large = lrg.name;\n          } else if (subject.level === 1) {\n            large = subject.name;\n          }\n        } else {\n          large = subjectId; // Fallback\n        }\n\n        courseRows.push({\n          courseId,\n          courseName: course.name,\n          largeSubject: large,\n          middleSubject: middle,\n          smallSubject: small,\n          mainHours: hours.main,\n          subHours: hours.sub,\n          totalHours: hours.main + hours.sub,\n          level: 2\n        });\n\n        courseTotalMain += hours.main;\n        courseTotalSub += hours.sub;\n      });\n\n      // Sort subjects: Large -> Middle -> Small\n      courseRows.sort((a, b) => \n        a.largeSubject.localeCompare(b.largeSubject) || \n        a.middleSubject.localeCompare(b.middleSubject) || \n        a.smallSubject.localeCompare(b.smallSubject)\n      );\n\n      // Add Course Header (optional, but requested Course subtotal)\n      // Actually, standard is Course | Subject | Main | Sub | Total\n      // Let's add all subject rows, then a Course subtotal row.\n      \n      rows.push(...courseRows);\n\n      rows.push({\n        courseId,\n        courseName: course.name,\n        largeSubject: '',\n        middleSubject: '',\n        smallSubject: t('Course Subtotal'),\n        mainHours: courseTotalMain,\n        subHours: courseTotalSub,\n        totalHours: courseTotalMain + courseTotalSub,\n        level: 3\n      });\n\n      grandTotalMain += courseTotalMain;\n      grandTotalSub += courseTotalSub;\n    });\n\n    return { rows, grandTotalMain, grandTotalSub };\n  }, [teacher, courses, subjects, lessons, periods, startDate, endDate]);\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"teacher-statistics-overlay\">\n      <div className=\"teacher-statistics-box\">\n        <div className=\"dialog-header\">\n          <h2>{t('Teacher Statistics')}: {teacher.name}</h2>\n          <div className=\"header-actions\">\n            <button \n              className=\"excel-export-btn\" \n              onClick={() => exportTeacherStatisticsToExcel({ \n                teacherName: teacher.name, \n                stats: stats.rows, \n                grandTotalMain: stats.grandTotalMain,\n                grandTotalSub: stats.grandTotalSub,\n                labels, t,\n                dateRange: startDate || endDate ? `${startDate} ~ ${endDate}` : t('All Period')\n              })}\n              title={t('Export to Excel')}\n              style={{ marginRight: '10px' }}\n            >\n              <svg width=\"18\" height=\"18\" viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\" fill=\"none\" stroke=\"currentColor\" stroke-width=\"2\" stroke-linecap=\"round\" stroke-linejoin=\"round\">\n                <path d=\"M21 15v4a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2v-4\"></path>\n                <polyline points=\"7 10 12 15 17 10\"></polyline>\n                <line x1=\"12\" y1=\"15\" x2=\"12\" y2=\"3\"></line>\n              </svg>\n              <span style={{ marginLeft: '5px' }}>Excel</span>\n            </button>\n            <button className=\"close-button\" onClick={onClose}>×</button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"teacher-statistics-content\">\n          <div className=\"range-selector\">\n            <label>{t('Period')}:</label>\n            <input type=\"date\" value={startDate} onChange={e => setStartDate(e.currentTarget.value)} />\n            <span>~</span>\n            <input type=\"date\" value={endDate} onChange={e => setEndDate(e.currentTarget.value)} />\n          </div>\n\n          <table className=\"stat-table\">\n            <thead>\n              <tr>\n                <th className=\"col-course\">{labels.course}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-large\">{labels.subjectLarge}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-middle\">{labels.subjectMiddle}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-small\">{labels.subjectSmall}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-main\">{labels.mainTeacher}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-sub\">{labels.subTeacher}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-total\">{t('Subtotal')}</th>\n              </tr>\n            </thead>\n            <tbody>\n              {stats.rows.map((row, idx) => {\n                const isFirstCourseRow = idx === 0 || stats.rows[idx-1].courseId !== row.courseId;\n                return (\n                  <tr key={`${row.courseId}-${idx}`} className={row.level === 3 ? 'course-subtotal' : ''}>\n                    <td className=\"col-course\">{isFirstCourseRow ? row.courseName : ''}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-large\">{row.largeSubject}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-middle\">{row.middleSubject}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-small\">{row.smallSubject}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-main\">{row.mainHours}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-sub\">{row.subHours}</td>\n                    <td className=\"col-total\">{row.totalHours}</td>\n                  </tr>\n                );\n              })}\n            </tbody>\n            <tfoot>\n              <tr className=\"grand-total\">\n                <td colSpan={4}>{t('Grand Total')}</td>\n                <td className=\"col-main\">{stats.grandTotalMain}</td>\n                <td className=\"col-sub\">{stats.grandTotalSub}</td>\n                <td className=\"col-total\">{stats.grandTotalMain + stats.grandTotalSub}</td>\n              </tr>\n            </tfoot>\n          </table>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"dialog-footer\">\n          <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={onClose}>{t('Close')}</button>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```

## MODEL ✨

**Conceiving Border Conditions** I'm currently focused on the logic needed to hide cell borders. The core challenge is establishing the criteria for removal. It hinges on the presence or absence of data in adjacent cells. If a 'nested subject' column is empty, the right border of its corresponding "parent" column should disappear. Now I must devise the method for detecting these empty adjacent cells.**Identifying Empty Cells** I've made headway, mapping out the specific column relationships. The logic to hide borders relies on adjacent cell emptiness, specifically: If the `col-middle` cell is empty, the right border of `col-large` should vanish. Similarly, empty `col-small` should trigger removal of the `col-middle` right border. The row.level value determines which column contains the content.**Revising Border Conditions** I'm now clarifying the implications of `row.level`. It dictates whether cells are rendered. When `row.level === 1`, only the `col-large` cell displays content, with `col-middle` and `col-small` being empty.  A level of 2 populates `col-middle`, and level 3 populates `col-small`. I believe hiding borders should correlate with these `row.level` values to create the span-like appearance the user desires.**Implementing the Border Logic** Now I have a clearer grasp of the rendering process and how levels interact. The core idea is that for level 1 rows, the borders of `col-large` and `col-middle` should be hidden, effectively spanning the content. Level 2 rows require the right border of `col-middle` to be hidden. I'm focusing on the CSS implications and how to inject these styles based on the row level to achieve the desired visual outcome.**Defining the Visual Span** The crucial insight is that the user wants a spanning effect. For level 1 rows, I'll hide the right borders of both `col-large` and `col-middle`. For level 2, the right border of `col-middle` needs to be hidden. I'm now focused on verifying that the CSS rules are applied correctly.**Defining Border Suppression Logic** I'm now establishing how to apply the `no-border-right` class. For level 1 rows, both `col-large` and `col-middle` will receive this class. For level 2 rows, only `col-middle` will get it. I'll focus on integrating these rules into the existing conditional rendering in `CourseStatistics.tsx` to achieve the intended spanning effect.**Implementing the Border Logic** Now, I've outlined the logic for conditional border removal, specifically focusing on `CourseStatistics.tsx`. I'll focus on applying the `no-border-right` class based on `row.level`. Level 1 rows will hide the right borders of `col-large` and `col-middle`, while level 2 rows will only hide the border of `col-middle`. ## MODEL ✨

**Analyzing Excel Export Issues** I'm currently investigating why `.no-border-top` isn't showing up in the Excel output for `CourseStatistics`. My focus is now on the `exportCourseStatisticsToExcel` function within `src/utils/excelExport.ts`. I will need to examine how the function manages the top borders to pinpoint the issue.**Examining CourseStatistics.tsx** I'm revisiting `CourseStatistics.tsx` to understand the conditions that trigger the "merged" or "aggregate" state for rows. I'm focusing on the `stat-level` and `stat-group/stat-leaf` classes to understand how the top borders should visually behave, especially for the "Assigned," "Scheduled," and "Diff" columns. The goal is to correlate the row's visual grouping with how borders are handled in the export function.**Correlating Border Conditions** I'm now cross-referencing the `stat-level` and `stat-group/stat-leaf` classes from `CourseStatistics.tsx` with the Excel export logic. The .no-border-top class is only applied to col-large and col-middle, but I need to ensure top borders are handled correctly for the Assigned, Scheduled, and Diff columns based on the grouping. It seems that if a row has the same large/middle subject then only the text gets hidden, but the "data" belongs to the "leaf" or is an aggregate.**Addressing Border Discrepancies** I've discovered the root cause. The `.no-border-top` class, central to this, is absent from the data columns, but is on the large/middle columns. If the row is "merged", the top border isn't removed from the data. I'm now adjusting the Excel export function to apply the `.no-border-top` style to the appropriate columns based on the 'stat-level' and 'stat-group/stat-leaf' classes used in `CourseStatistics.tsx`. I need to ensure all rows are handled appropriately based on if a row is a continuation.**Refining Excel Border Logic** I'm revisiting the border logic in `exportCourseStatisticsToExcel`. The current implementation in `src/utils/excelExport.ts` correctly handles top borders for the large and middle columns. The crucial detail is that the `no-border-top` class in `CourseStatistics.tsx` is only applied to the `col-large` and `col-middle` columns. I need to make adjustments to apply `.no-border-top` to the other columns as well, when required.**Refining Export Function Analysis** I'm now fully immersed in the `exportCourseStatisticsToExcel` function. Admin role required.' });\n  }\n  const { id } = req.params;\n  try {\n    // Get original course (including related subjects and sub teachers)\n    const original = await prisma.resource.findUnique({\n      where: { id },\n      include: {\n        subjects: true,\n        assistantTeachers: true\n      }\n    });\n\n    if (!original || original.type !== ResourceType.course) {\n      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Course not found' });\n    }\n\n    // Create new course (using transaction)\n    const duplicated = await prisma.$transaction(async (tx) => {\n      // 1. Create new course resource\n      const newCourse = await tx.resource.create({\n        data: {\n          name: `(Copy) ${original.name}`,\n          type: ResourceType.course,\n          order: (original.order || 0) + 1, // Place at next position of original course\n          startDate: original.startDate,\n          endDate: original.endDate,\n          mainRoomId: original.mainRoomId,\n          chiefTeacherId: original.chiefTeacherId,\n          mainTeacherLabel: original.mainTeacherLabel,\n          subTeacherLabel: original.subTeacherLabel,\n          assistantTeachers: {\n            connect: original.assistantTeachers.map(t => ({ id: t.id }))\n          }\n        }\n      });\n\n      // 2. Clone subjects\n      if (original.subjects.length > 0) {\n        await tx.courseSubject.createMany({\n          data: original.subjects.map(s => ({\n            name: s.name,\n            totalPeriods: s.totalPeriods,\n            resourceId: newCourse.id\n          }))\n        });\n      }\n\n      return await tx.resource.findUnique({\n        where: { id: newCourse.id },\n        include: { subjects: true, assistantTeachers: true }\n      });\n    });\n\n    res.json(duplicated);\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error('Failed to duplicate course:', error);\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to duplicate course' });\n  }\n});\n\n// Clone lessons between courses (ADMIN / Course Chief or Assistant Teacher)\napp.post('/api/courses/:id/duplicate-lessons', verifyToken, async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {\n  if (!req.user) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Not authenticated' });\n  const { id: destinationCourseId } = req.params;\n  const { sourceCourseId, startDate, endDate } = req.body;"
```json
  }
```
```json
}
```

## MODEL ✨

I've fixed the `Duplicate Course` logic and improved the visual grouping in `CourseStatistics` and `TeacherStatistics` by hiding redundant borders. I'll now provide the user with a summary of these changes.

### 1. Statistics Border Improvements (UI & Excel)
*   **CSS `border-collapse` Challenge:** Standard tables struggle with `border-top: none` when a previous row has `border-bottom`.
*   **Solution:**
    *   Switched to `border-top` as the primary row separator for data rows.
    *   Used `border-top: hidden !important` for the `.no-border-top` class to override collapsed borders.
    *   Implemented hierarchical tracking (Large -> Middle -> Small) to selectively apply `.no-border-top`, `.no-border-left`, and `.no-border-right`. This hides internal grid lines when items belong to the same parent or adjacent cells are empty, creating a "spanned" look.
*   **Excel Export:** Mirrored this logic in `excelExport.ts` by selectively drawing `top`, `left`, and `right` borders while omitting the default `bottom` border to achieve the same visual grouping in `.xlsx` files.

### 2. Course Duplication Logic (Backend)
*   **Context:** With the new `Subject Manager`, courses now belong to a `Course Type` and link to hierarchical `Subjects` via `subjectId`.
*   **Improvements:**
    *   **`courseTypeId`:** Now correctly cloned to the new course.
    *   **`CourseSubject` structure:** Fixed the duplication to include `subjectId`. This ensures the cloned course retains its hierarchical relationship to the master subject tree, allowing for accurate statistics and filtering.
    *   **Naming:** Changed suffix to `(Copy)` for better readability.

These updates ensure both visual clarity in reports and data integrity when managing courses and subjects. I'm finished.

## MODEL ✨

The overlap logic `sStart <= eEnd && eStart <= sEnd` is flawed, as it incorrectly checks `eStart` against `sEnd`. It should be `sStart <= eEnd && eStart <= sEnd`. Wait, that's what I just said. Let's re-read: `return sStart <= eEnd && eStart <= sEnd;`. `eStart` is from `existingLesson`, `sEnd` is from `sourceLesson`. The correct interval overlap check is `max(start1, start2) <= min(end1, end2)`, which translates to `sStart <= eEnd && eStart <= sEnd`. This matches what's there. My mistake. It's correct. I'm done.

I have updated the lesson duplication logic to correctly handle the new hierarchical subject structure.

### Key Improvement

*   **`subjectId` Handling:** When cloning lessons from one course to another, the `subjectId` is now explicitly copied. This ensures that the cloned lessons remain linked to the correct master subject in the tree, which is essential for accurate statistics and filtering.

Combined with the previous updates to Course Duplication, the system now fully respects the `Course Type` and `Subject Tree` hierarchy when performing management operations.

## MODEL ✨

I have updated `src/i18n.ts` to use a relative path for loading translation files. By removing the leading slash from `loadPath`, i18next will now fetch the locale JSON files relative to the location of `index.html`. This ensures the application functions correctly even when it is not served from the root of the domain.

    "output": "\nIMPORTANT: The file content has been truncated.\nStatus: Showing lines 105-115 of 183 total lines.\nAction: To read more of the file, you can use the 'start_line' and 'end_line' parameters in a subsequent 'read_file' call. For example, to read the next section of the file, use start_line: 116.\n\n--- FILE CONTENT (truncated) ---\n            {row.level === 2 ? row.name : ''}\n          </td>\n          <td className={`col-small ${row.level <= 2 ? 'no-border-left' : ''}`}>\n            {row.level === 3 ? row.name : ''}\n          </td>\n          <td className=\"col-assigned\">{row.assigned}</td>\n          <td className=\"col-scheduled\">{row.scheduled}</td>\n          <td className=\"col-diff\">\n            <span className={row.scheduled > row.assigned ? 'text-over' : row.scheduled < row.assigned ? 'text-under' : ''}>\n              {row.scheduled - row.assigned}\n            </span>"
```json
  }
}
```

---

## MODEL ✨

`Teacher Statistics`のタイトル表示を動的な `labels.teacher` を使用するように変更し、翻訳ファイルにも対応するキーを追加しました。これで、管理画面の設定で講師リソースの表示名を変更しても、統計画面のタイトルに正しく反映されるようになります。
